    type options struct {
  port *int
}

type Option func(options *options) error

func WithPort(port int) Option {
  return func(options *options) error {
    if port < 0 {
    return errors.New("port should be positive")
  }
  options.port = &port
  return nil
  }
}

func NewServer(addr string, opts ...Option) ( *http.Server, error) {
  var options options
  for _, opt := range opts { 
    err := opt(&options) 
    if err != nil {
      return nil, err
    }
  }

// ã“ã®æ®µéšã§ã€options æ§‹é€ ä½“ãŒæ§‹ç¯‰ã•ã‚Œã€æ§‹æˆãŒå«ã¾ã‚Œã¾ã™ã€‚
// ã—ãŸãŒã£ã¦ã€ãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆè¨­å®šã«é–¢é€£ã™ã‚‹ãƒ­ã‚¸ãƒƒã‚¯ã‚’å®Ÿè£…ã§ãã¾ã™ã€‚
  var port int
  if options.port == nil {
    port = defaultHTTPPort
  } else {
      if *options.port == 0 {
      port = randomPort()
    } else {
      port = *options.port
    }
  }

    func concat(values []string) string {

    defer notify(status)
    defer incrementCounter(status)

    }
